\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ .HOUR, }\DataTypeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ .GENERAL_SUPPLY_KWH, }\DataTypeTok{group =}\NormalTok{ DATE, }\DataTypeTok{colour =}\NormalTok{ Weekend)) }\OperatorTok{+}

\begin{Shaded}

\KeywordTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{#training and test set}
\NormalTok{trainIndex <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{createDataPartition}\NormalTok{(EnergyDataAggregate}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{GENERAL_SUPPLY_KWH, }\DataTypeTok{p =} \FloatTok{.5}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{list =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{times =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{energyData.train=EnergyDataAggregate[trainIndex,]}
\NormalTok{energyData.test=EnergyDataAggregate[}\OperatorTok{-}\NormalTok{trainIndex,]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
